< Text>
The New York taco is my favorite.  Pepino,  elote, ceviche,  and spicy shrimp tacos are good too.  Nice place to watch sports and have a cold beer with good food.  Service is not so great.  They play a good music selection. We took family out on a Wednesday due to an ad on Facebook that the manager did not honor.  It says, Kids eat free. Buy a meal, get a kids meal free. (see picture)  When we ordered our waitress confirmed with the manager that only 1 kids meal was free per table, per family.  I call it false advertising.  My wife and I took our 3 kids hoping to take advantage of the ad and get two free kids meals. They wouldn't budge.  Very misleading ad.   Food is good though.<//Text>

My wife and I live in walking distance so we do not get the benefit of the parking validation. The prices are good.  We've encountered a few technical difficulties since going here.  Once the movie lights remained on until someone told the staff. Another time the sound didn't trigger until the staff was notified. <rating>3< /rating>< Text>
My mom lives here. It's well-kept, but the HOA fees keep going up and up, currently at $850 a month! She doesn't golf and isn't super active for medical reasons, so she's not getting her money's worth from that. There is a broken sewer line right outside her unit that backs up into her bathtub on holidays when everyone has guests, and they are not being proactive about fixing it. They could do better. But overall, it's safe, it's attractive, and they have lots of activities for those who can participate. Would be nice to have a lower rate for those who aren't able to.</Text>
